<rate>2<//rate>< Review>
Genuine company although misleading job postings. I understand their goals and what type of talent they are attempting to attract. However, the job postings are VERY misleading. The market manager positions are actualy field marketing representatives, representing brands in store and selling services to consumers. The pay is directed at very entry level candidates.

The recruiter I spoke with was very helpful and informative and she did a great job. However, from our first call the position seemed more of an actual marketing manager working with brands to achieve maximum ROI through marketing campaigns and overseeing several campaigns across multiple brands. Upon my second call back I mentioned I read these reviews and she was much more transparent in what the job actually was. Although theres nothing wrong with the position, it was misleading. Hence, the guy that pulled up in his Tesla(from another reviwe here) thinking it was a career advancement opportunity.

The company is 100% legit and not a scam, HOWEVER your recruiting department has some work to do in presenting the job as what it is. Had you presented the job correctly, you'd see a lot less negative reviews. For those seeking a first job or would like to transition from retail into brand marketing, this is the job for you. For those who are already in marketing, are managers, and have experience in field marketing, this is NOT the job for you. And to be clear i'm talking about the Marketing Manager position ONLY, as that was the position I was initially interested in and was in discussion with the recruiter.<//Review>

This is excellent customer service and they are to be commended for the follow up and ultimately how they handled the problem. As a carpenter with 35+ years experience I can tell you the quality of these doors is exceptional and I assume the balance of their inventory is equally as well-built. <Review>I used their doors & drawer faces to remodel a 1980's kitchen using the original ugly dark brown cabinets. Their doors are an almost exact match to the current cabinets being sold at the big box hardware stores. They are at least the same quality, but I actually think they are higher quality. Their support people helped me find the correct edge profile (there are many, but there are only a few that are really popular at the big box stores right now). The items came quicker than I expected. The big box stores no longer offer this service where you can order doors only. I saved money by buying my hinges locally, and bored my own concealed hinge holes. This also allowed me to choose between 1/2 and 3/4" offset on my old cabinet frames, as I wasn't exactly sure how the doors would lay out. I ended up using 1/2" offset and one door at the end is 3/4" offset. They look perfect, like the factory.<//Review>< Pics>
